<a id="27814" href="Frame.html#27749" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a> <a id="27832" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="27834" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#2442" class="Function">SNS‚ÜíUnivalentStr</a> <a id="27851" href="Frame.html#25220" class="Function">isHomoEqv</a> <a id="27861" href="Frame.html#27307" class="Function">frame-is-SNS</a>

<a id="27875" class="Comment">-- Similar to the poset case, this is sufficient to establish that the category of frames</a>
<a id="27965" class="Comment">-- is univalent</a>

<a id="‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°"></a><a id="27982" href="Frame.html#27982" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="27987" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27989" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="27990" href="Frame.html#27990" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="27992" href="Frame.html#27992" class="Bound">G</a> <a id="27994" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="27996" href="Frame.html#3701" class="Function">Frame</a> <a id="28002" href="Basis.html#2455" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="28005" href="Basis.html#2458" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="28008" href="Basis.html#2461" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÇ</a><a id="28010" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28012" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="28014" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28015" href="Frame.html#27990" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28017" href="Frame.html#25460" class="Function Operator">‚âÉf</a> <a id="28020" href="Frame.html#27992" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28021" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28023" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Glue.html#1051" class="Function Operator">‚âÉ</a> <a id="28025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28026" href="Frame.html#27990" class="Bound">F</a> <a id="28028" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="28030" href="Frame.html#27992" class="Bound">G</a><a id="28031" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="28033" href="Frame.html#27982" class="Function">‚âÉf‚âÉ‚â°</a> <a id="28038" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="28040" href="Cubical.Foundations.SIP.html#4416" class="Function">SIP</a> <a id="28044" href="Frame.html#27749" class="Function">frame-is-univ-str</a>

<a id="28063" class="Comment">-- However, there are two minor issues with this.</a>
<a id="28113" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28116" class="Comment">--   1. We do not have to talk about equivalences as we are talking about sets;</a>
<a id="28196" class="Comment">--      isomorphisms are well-behaved in our case as we are dealing with sets.</a>
<a id="28275" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28278" class="Comment">--  2. We do not have to require the frame data to be preserved. We can show that any</a>
<a id="28364" class="Comment">--     poset isomorphism preserves the frame operators.</a>
<a id="28420" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="28423" class="Comment">-- We will therefore strengthen our result to work with the notion of poset isomorphism.</a>

<a id="28513" class="Comment">-- We start by showing the equivalence between ‚âÉf and ‚âÖ‚Çö.</a>

<a id="34014" class="Comment">-- Now that we have this result, we can move on to show that given two frames F and G,</a>
<a id="34101" class="Comment">-- (pos F) ‚âÖ‚Çö (pos G) is equivalent to F ‚â° G.</a>
